Chinese Educational Society: Held Fifth Board Meeting Yesterday; Compiling and Printing Research Results on Production Education and Teacher Training; Academic Year Length for Winter and Summer Vacations, and Sundays Should Remain Unchanged; —Petitioning the Ministry of Education to Explain the Phonetic Alphabet and Temporarily Suspend Implementation— 189

The Chinese Educational Society held its fifth board meeting yesterday (the 7th) at the Shanghai Provincial High School. Many important cases were resolved. The reporter from the Shen Shi News Agency presents the details as follows:

Board Members Present: Yang Lianggong, Chang Daozhi, Xu Keshi, Du Zuozhou, (Chairman) Chen Lijiang, Zheng Xigu, (Recorder) Ou Yuanhuai, Chen Jianxiao, Tao Heng, Meng Xiancheng, Xie Xunchu, Zheng Xiaocang, Chen Heqin, Cheng Qibao, (Zheng - acting)

Reported Items: (1) Board member Chen Jianxiao reported on the society's joining the World Education Fellowship and reported on the previous board meeting's recommendation of Tao Xingzhi to negotiate the assets of the Chinese Education Improvement Society. (2) Board member Xu Keshi reported on funding and group membership matters. (3) Board member Yang Lianggong reported on investigating the catalog of educational books. (4) Board member He Shuangqiu reported on the research results of production education.

Matters for Discussion: (1) How to urge the progress of the society's central research issues in order to complete them before the annual meeting. Resolution: (A) Ask each responsible committee to be responsible for completing them on schedule. (B) Publish the research results of production education as a separate publication. (2) Should the society publish a special education issue before the annual meeting? Resolution: A. Publish a special issue on teacher training. Request the Educational Magazine to print it on behalf of the society. The society will nominate a committee to be responsible for editing. B. Nominate Zheng Xiaocang, Zhuang Zeyi, and Shen Yougan to be responsible for editing, with the assistance of Ou Yuanhuai and Zheng Xigu, convened by Zhuang Zeyi. C. Ask Ou Yuanhuai and Zheng Xigu to contact the Educational Magazine. Each board member of the society should contribute at least one article. (3) What opinions does the society have on curriculum issues? Resolution: Nominate Ao Maoru, Chen Heqin, Zhuang Zeyi, Zheng Xigu, and Cui Zaiyang to first collect materials and submit them for discussion at the annual meeting, convened by Chen Heqin. (4) How to promote universal education? Resolution: Nominate Tao Xingzhi, Tai Shuangqiu, Chen Yimin, Xu Keshi, and Wu Yanyin to be responsible for collecting and deliberating on concrete plans for universal education, convened by Tao Xingzhi. (5) Regarding the attention to the issue of Chinese characters, what opinions does the society want to express? Resolution: Submit a report to the Ministry of Education explaining that the phonetic alphabet is detrimental to learning efficiency, eyesight, printing, hygiene, and economy. Before there are experimental results, its implementation should be temporarily suspended to show caution. Also, explain that the society has now nominated Chen Heqin, Chen Lijiang, Shen Yougan, Tao Xingzhi, Zhou Xiangeng, Ai Xizhou, Zhang Yi, Hu Yi, and Du Zuozhou to first engage in experimental work separately, and report again after there are results. (6) Send a letter to the Zhejiang Secondary Education Research Society expressing sympathy for the cancellation of graduation exams, and request that the materials from the canceled exams be sent to the society for reference. (7) What opinions does the society have on shortening the length of schooling? Resolution: A. The number of weekdays should not be reduced. B. Winter and summer vacations and the length of schooling should not be shortened, but time during the vacation should be used as much as possible for extracurricular educational activities, such as summer schools, youth association services, and group travel. (8) Regarding how to maintain the education bureau system, Resolution: Publicly nominate Yang Lianggong and Tai Shuangqiu to be responsible for planning detailed concrete methods and submit them for discussion at the next board meeting. (9) How should the society collect membership fees? Resolution: Local membership fees will be collected by local branches and remitted to the headquarters. (10) Regarding the date and location of the annual meeting, the resolution was that the annual meeting will be held on July 11, 12, and 13 at Beijing Normal University. The Beijing branch will be responsible for preparation. (11) The China Children's Education Society requested to jointly hold the annual meeting with the society and to co-sponsor a summer training course. Resolution: The society and the Children's Education Society will jointly hold an opening ceremony on the morning of July 11, and then hold separate meetings in stages. As for the summer training course, the society has various difficulties and cannot hold it, so please have Beijing Normal University consider planning it. (12) The Beijing branch requested the allocation of funds for the old problem of the research society. Resolution: The society will subsidize 100 yuan. (13) Should the society's membership directory be reprinted? Resolution: Reprint it and have it printed before the annual meeting. (14) Regarding the introduction of new members, Resolution: Hand it over to Yang Lianggong, Xu Keshi, Xie Xunchu, and Zheng Xigu for separate review, and then submit it to the next board meeting.

Public Notice to Members: Shanghai branch members held a public banquet for all board members on the 9th floor of the Youth Association last night (the 7th) at 7:00 PM. More than 20 people attended, including Liu Zhanen, Ou Yuanou, Ge Liting, Shao Shuangqiu, Shu Xincheng, and Zheng Xigu. There was much toasting and lively discussion. Guests and hosts all enjoyed themselves. Board members from other places are all scheduled to leave Shanghai today, it is said.

Jiangsu Central Schools Anti-Smoking Speech Finals: 18 Selected for Preliminaries... 5 Selected for Free Competition 190

(Zhenjiang News) The Jiangsu Provincial Anti-Smoking Association held the provincial middle school student anti-smoking speech competition. The preliminaries began at 2:00 PM on the 6th at Zhenjiang Normal School. There were 55 official contestants, divided into 6 groups. To avoid burying talent among the councilors exceeding the quota of each school (one person stipulated per unit), a separate free competition group was temporarily opened. 18 people participated and 5 were selected. First place: Liu Tongsheng from Jiangsu Yangzhou Middle School; Second place: Zhang Chuanlian from Jiangsu Yangzhou Middle School; Third place: Fan Zuzhu from Nantong Middle School; Fourth place: Wu Tingzuo from Qixia Rural Normal School; Fifth place: Gu Fengxiang from Jiangsu Yangzhou Middle School. The above five are the winners of the finals and may no longer participate in the preliminary round of the official group of the overall finals. Three people were selected from each group, and the finals will be held at 2:00 PM on the 7th in the auditorium of the Provincial Party Headquarters, and prizes will be awarded on the spot. The results of the preliminaries are as follows: Group 1: Ge Peifen (Taicang Normal), Sun Kai (Huaian Middle), He Maoxun (Yangzhou Middle); Group 2: Hu Yanfu (Huaiyin Agricultural), Feng Yiwu (Donghai Normal), Fa Dongzuo (Zhenjiang Normal); Group 3: Ji Zhuangnan (Nantong), Zhang Shubao (Beijing Girls' Middle), Lu Xianyu (Xuzhou Middle); Group 4: Sun Yongzhang (Tongzhou Middle), Gao Yiding (Su Agricultural), Sun Defang (Xuzhou Women's Normal); Group 5: Shen Fuyao (Huangdu Rural Normal), Peng Kunyuan (Songjiang Girls' Middle), Chen Shanji (Jiangdu); Group 6: Tong Yichang (Yunhe Rural Normal), Ji Baozhang (Danyang), Kong Xiangshu (Nanjing Middle).

China Educational Film Association: Shanghai Branch Held Annual Meeting Yesterday; Headquarters and Party and Government Organs Sent Representatives to Give Instructions; Tong Hangbai, Pan Gongzhan, and Others Elected as Directors and Supervisors 191

The Shanghai branch of the China Educational Film Association held its second annual meeting at the Municipal Public Education Hall at 2:00 PM yesterday. More than 90 members attended. Details are recorded as follows:

Members Present: Including Pan Gongzhan, Tong Hangbai, Li Zhaohuan, Jiang Jianbai, Chen Bai, Yang Minshi, Zheng Zhengqiu, Xu Gongmei, Zheng Xiaoqiu, Yuan Zengyu, Chen Songchun, Shi Pengnian, Wu Bangfan, Ding Shouting, Lu Hailan, Hu Jiheng, and other ninety people. Pan Gongzhan, representative of the headquarters, Mao Yun, representative of the Municipal Party Department, and Nie Haifan, representative of the Municipal Education Bureau, attended and gave instructions.

Annual Meeting Situation: The meeting opened at 2:00 PM. The presidium was Pan Gongzhan, Chen Bai, and Zheng Zhengqiu, the recorder was Shi Pengnian, and the master of ceremonies was Yuan Zengyu. After the usual formalities, Chairman Zheng Zhengqiu first reported on the association's affairs, followed by speeches from Pan Gongzhan, representative of the headquarters, Mao Yun, representative of the Municipal Party Department, and Nie Haifan, representative of the Municipal Education Bureau. Then, proposals were discussed, and officials were elected. The meeting adjourned after a group photo.

Pan's Speech: Mr. Pan Gongzhan, representing the headquarters, gave a speech saying, "Today, the Shanghai branch of the China Educational Film Association is holding its second annual meeting. In the past two years, whether from the perspective of career or membership, the Shanghai branch can be seen as the most powerful branch in the entire organization of the China Educational Film Association. I hope you will continue to work hard to reach the headquarters' expectations for the Shanghai branch. However, when we review the past, there is one point that should be noted, that is, the members who joined the Shanghai branch are mostly from the film industry, and fewer from the education field. This proves that the Shanghai education field has not yet recognized the effectiveness of film in education, so they cannot be interested in the association and maintain a cold attitude, making it very difficult to promote our work. The reason is that we cannot shirk our responsibility for the educational films we show not being satisfactory. Therefore, in the future, I hope the film industry will take more responsibility, produce domestically made educational films, and cooperate with the education field to make them suitable for the needs of Chinese students," and so on.

Discussion of Proposals: One proposal: Regarding a matter discussed at the third joint meeting of the executive and supervisory committee of the second session of the branch, that the branch should establish a fund management committee to raise funds, but there is no such provision in the constitution, so a clause should be added to the constitution. It is proposed to pass it and then submit it to the annual meeting for ratification. Resolution: Add a clause to Chapter 3 of the constitution: "This branch may establish special committees when necessary, and the detailed rules will be formulated separately," etc. recorded in the minutes. Now, a special request is made for ratification. Resolution: Approve the ratification.

Election Results: This session adopted a postal election. The ballots were opened in public yesterday. As a result, Tong Hangbai, Jiang Jianbai, Chen Heqin, Li Zhaohua, Zhou Jianyun, Yang Minshi, and Lu Shibai were elected as directors. Gao Tianlou, Chen Songchun, Yao Sufeng, and Tao Bosun are alternates. Pan Gongzhan, Wu Kaixian, Chen Bai, Zheng Zhengqiu, and Xu Gongmei are supervisors. Jin Jingyu, Shao Zuiweng, and Bu Wancang are alternates.

World Student Association Inquiries About the Arrest of Students in Japan; Students in Japan Always Maintain Discipline; Unjust Arrests Are Intolerable Under Public Law 192

Recently, it was telegraphed that the puppet Puyi went to Japan, Japanese detectives were all over the key transportation points, and a large number of Chinese students in Japan were unjustly arrested. The Zhonghua Student Association was also surrounded and searched. These phenomena occurred amidst the expulsion of overseas Chinese from Japan, which is unfortunate. It is understood that the World Student Association in Shanghai has sent a letter to students in Japan to inquire about the truth in order to negotiate. It is found that under the management and leadership of Minister Jiang and Supervisor Zhou, Chinese students in Japan have always been quite disciplined. Now, unjust arrests are truly intolerable under international public law.

Sponsored by the Chinese Cultural Construction Association: National Reading Movement Conference Opens; From Today to the 21st; All Bookstores Voluntarily Sell Books at a 50% Discount; Chen Lifu and Wu Xingya to Broadcast in Beijing and Shanghai 193

In order to create a national atmosphere of learning and promote cultural standards, the Chinese Cultural Construction Association, in addition to holding a reading competition, will also hold a National Reading Movement Conference from April 8 to April 21. Details are recorded as follows:

Opening Today: The National Reading Movement Conference is scheduled to open today. During these two weeks, all major publishing institutions in the country will uniformly sell books at low prices for the sake of the reading movement. Most of the books in this edition are sold at a 50% discount. Various magazines are also specially priced. All major primary and secondary schools across the country will hold a Reading Movement Commemorative Week during these two weeks, guiding students on reading methods. Major newspapers will also issue reading problem guidance, written mostly by famous figures in the academic world.

Celebrity Lectures: Starting from the 8th, the Chinese Cultural Construction Association has specially hired Wu Tiecheng, Wu Xingya, Wang Yunwu, Cai Jiemin, Tao Baichuan, Weng Zhilong, Sun Hanbing, Zhang Sumin, Fan Zhongyun, He Bingsong, Wang Xinming, Pan Gongzhan, Zhang Yuanruo, Zhang Yousan and other fourteen people to give lectures on various reading-related topics. From 8:20 AM to 9:00 AM today, Chairman Chen Lifu of the association will broadcast the "Opening Address of the National Reading Movement Conference" on the Nanjing Central Broadcasting Station. Wu Xingya will broadcast "Reading Problems and the Chinese Revolution" on the Shanghai Sino-Western Broadcasting Station from 3:15 PM to 3:30 PM this afternoon.

Education Bureau Notice: The Municipal Education Bureau issued a notice to the schools in this city yesterday, stating, "Approved by the Chinese Cultural Construction Association's official letter stating, 'We are launching a National Reading Competition and Reading Movement Conference to correct the bad habits of youth being arrogant, extravagant, and abandoning learning, and to create a good learning atmosphere. In addition to the Reading Competition, which has already started on the 25th of this month, the Reading Movement Conference is also planned to be held for two weeks from April 8 to April 21. We have obtained the full support of the publishing and news industries in this city and other places, either by issuing special publications or holding special low prices. We have always admired your bureau's efforts in cultural work and presiding over education. For this reason, we intend to ask you to order all levels of schools in the city to simultaneously hold Reading Movement Week during the period of the reading movement held by our association, and to hold student reading speech competitions to facilitate publicity and encouragement. We would be grateful if you would grant this request. In addition to the reading movement slogans, which will be sent by our association separately, this matter concerns encouraging youth and we hope that you will agree to it,' etc. Approved, it is deemed that the letter requests the notification of all items, which concern encouraging youth and promoting cultural construction, and should be handled accordingly. In addition to the separate letter, we hereby order the said school to comply with the instructions."

Shaanxi Army Spring Games to be Held in Mid-May

Yang Hucheng Promotes Sports in Shaanxi Province; Shaanxi Army Spring Games to be Held in Mid-May 195

(Xi'an News, Xi'an 6th) Director Yang Hucheng believes that sports in Shaanxi Province have always been extremely backward, and that saving the country and the nation is based on sports. Now, he has decided to actively promote it among the soldiers first. He has recently asked experts to formulate various measures and issued orders to all troops to implement them. It is also scheduled to hold the Spring Games of various troops in Xi'an in mid-May when the weather is sunny. All Shaanxi troops are preparing to participate, it is said.

Zhang Boling and Ma John Arrive in Shanghai 197

(Nanjing 7th) Ma John, director of physical education at Tsinghua University, and Zhang Boling, president of Nankai University, arrived in Nanjing by train from Pinghu. They did not stay when they passed through Nanjing on the evening of the 7th. They arrived in Shanghai to attend the preparatory meeting of the National Games. After the meeting, they will participate in the Physical Education Committee of the Ministry of Education. Mr. Ma will return to Peiping after the meeting is over. Mr. Zhang must come to Nanjing for a trip and will stay for a few days, it is said.

Jiangwan Cross-Country Race: Athletes from Various Teams Participate in the Competition; Total of 15 Teams with More Than 130 People; We will Devote all our Efforts to Organize a Strong Team to Compete 198

The annual Jiangwan cross-country race is scheduled to be held on the 14th of this month and has been reported in this newspaper. The Shanghai Athletics Competition Promotion Association, in view of the fact that the last time the Chinese team suffered a complete defeat, was due to the dispersion of famous players among various teams. Therefore, there was a proposal to organize a strong team. Since the competition date is approaching, the association held an executive meeting a few days ago. Bai Hongkang Kongzhao, Zhonghua Sun Zhifei Chong, Huaguang Kang Taiming, and Post Office Xu Duo attended. At that time, it was decided that Sun Zhichong would be responsible for planning. It is now understood that the selection of players has been carefully reviewed and with the permission of each person, it has been decided to divide the team into two teams, A and B. Team A includes Wu Hanzhang, He Baoshan, Jin Zhongkang, Wang Zhilin, Zhang Liang, and Gu Huaiyuan. Team B includes Wan Jinsheng, Huang Rulin, Yang Guangxie, Lan Shijie, Zhou Ruquan, and Ji Yongqing. At that time, they will represent the Shanghai Joint Team to attend the finals. The participants this time include Shanghai Joint Team A and B, Ennis A, B, C, and D, French Army A and B, West Sports Association A and B, Zhonghua Sports Association Huaguang Track and Field Team, Hongkou Cross-Country Team, and Russian Overseas Chinese Huasers, one team each, a total of fifteen teams, and about 20 individual participants. There are more than 130 athletes in total, which is more than 20 more than the previous session. Also, the date set by the association will still be held as usual even if it is cloudy and rainy. The association also notified the Hongkou Cross-Country Team to quickly send the list to Sun Zhichong at the General Motor Vehicle Department on the third floor of the Fourth Road Police Station for printing, it is said.
